# <a name="dimensions-and-measures-available-in-call-quality-dashboard"></a><span data-ttu-id="29eb2-103">通話品質儀表板中提供的維度與量值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-103">Dimensions and measures available in Call Quality Dashboard</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-104">Microsoft 團隊和商務用 Skype Online 的通話品質儀表板 (CQD) 可讓您深入瞭解使用 Microsoft 團隊和商務用 Skype 服務所進行的通話品質。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-104">The Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online allows you to gain insights into the quality of calls made using Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business services.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-105">本主題提供 CQD 所公開之維度與量值的詳細資訊。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-105">This topic provides detailed information about the dimensions and measures exposed by CQD.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-106">若要深入瞭解 CQD 及如何啟用它, 請參閱[開啟與使用 Microsoft 團隊和商務用 Skype Online 的通話品質儀表板](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-106">To learn more about CQD and how to enable it, see [Turning on and using Call Quality Dashboard for Microsoft Teams and Skype for Business Online](turning-on-and-using-call-quality-dashboard.md).</span></span>



## <a name="first-and-second-endpoint-classification"></a><span data-ttu-id="29eb2-107">第一和第二個端點分類</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-107">First and Second endpoint classification</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-108">通話品質儀表板 (CQD) 中的許多維度與量值標示為第一個或第二個。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-108">Many of the dimensions and measures in Call Quality Dashboard (CQD) are labeled as first or second.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-109">下列邏輯會判斷資料流程或呼叫中所涉及的端點標示為「第一」:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-109">The following logic determines which endpoint involved in the stream or call is labeled as first:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-110">首先會是伺服器端點 (AV MCU、中繼伺服器等)。如果您的伺服器是在串流/通話中參與。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-110">First will always be a Server endpoint (AV MCU, Mediation Server, etc.) if a Server is involved in the stream/call.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-111">第二個將一直是用戶端端點, 除非資料流程位於兩個伺服器端點之間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-111">Second will always be a Client endpoint unless the stream is between two Server endpoints.</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-112">如果兩個端點都是相同的類型, 則第一個與第二個端點的順序是以使用者代理程式類別的內部排序為基礎。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-112">If both endpoints are the same type, the order for which is first vs. second is based on internal ordering of the user agent category.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-113">這可確保順序一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-113">This ensures the ordering is consistent.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-114">例如, 每個資料列代表一個資料流程中所涉及的一組使用者代理程式:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-114">For example, each row represents a pair of User Agents involved in a stream:</span></span>

||||||
|:-----|:-----|:-----|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-115">**來電者的使用者代理類別**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-115">**User Agent Category of Caller**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-116">**被呼叫者的使用者代理類別**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-116">**User Agent Category of Callee**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-117">**第一個端點**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-117">**First Endpoint**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-118">**第二個端點**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-118">**Second Endpoint**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-119">**首先是來電者**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-119">**First Is Caller**</span></span> <br/> |

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-154">第一和第二種分類是獨立于來電者或被叫商的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-154">That First and Second classification is separate from which endpoint is the caller or callee.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-155">第一個是呼叫方維度可用來協助找出哪個端點是呼叫者或被叫方。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-155">The First Is Caller dimension can be used to help identify which endpoint was the caller or callee.</span></span>

## <a name="dimensions"></a><span data-ttu-id="29eb2-156">三維</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-156">Dimensions</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-167">第一個網路名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-167">First Network Name</span></span>  <br/>                                         | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-168">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-168">String</span></span>  <br/>                         | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-169">根據將子網傳到入口網站的租使用者建立資料的第一個端點, 在媒體資料流程中使用的網路名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-169">Name of network used for media stream by first endpoint based on mapping subnet to tenant building data uploaded to portal.</span></span>  <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                        | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-170">空白值表示端點未報告的網路資料, 或網路沒有在子網對應資料中定義的網路名稱。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-170">Blank values indicate network data not reported by the endpoint or network does not have network name defined in subnet mapping data.</span></span>   <br/> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-171">**範例值:** 美國/華盛頓/雷蒙德</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-171">**Example value:** USA/ WA/ REDMOND</span></span>  <br/>                                                                                                                            |

| <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-177">第一個建築物名稱</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-177">First Building Name</span></span>  <br/>                                        | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-178">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-178">String</span></span>  <br/>                         | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-179">第一個端點所在之建築物的名稱, 此基礎是根據將子網對應至租使用者將資料上傳到入口網站的租使用者。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-179">Name of the building where the first endpoint was located based on mapping subnet to tenant building data uploaded to portal.</span></span>  <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                      | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-180">空白值表示端點未報告的網路資料, 網路不在商業網路中, 或網路沒有在子網對應資料中定義的「建築物名稱」。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-180">Blank values indicate network data not reported by the endpoint, network is not within corporate network or network does not have building name defined in subnet mapping data.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-181">**範例值:** 主</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-181">**Example value:** Main</span></span>  <br/>                                                                                               |
| <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-182">第一次擁有權類型</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-182">First Ownership Type</span></span>  <br/>                                       | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-183">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-183">String</span></span>  <br/>                         | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-184">第一個端點所在之組建的擁有權類型, 其基礎系是根據將子網上傳到入口網站的租使用者建立資料。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-184">Ownership type of building where the first endpoint was located based on mapping subnet to tenant building data uploaded to portal.</span></span>  <br/>                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                                | <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-185">空白值表示端點未報告的網路資料, 網路不在商業網路中, 或網路沒有在子網對應資料中定義擁有權。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-185">Blank values indicate network data not reported by the endpoint, network is not within corporate network or network does not have ownership defined in subnet mapping data.</span></span> <br/>  <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-186">**範例值:** Contoso-IT</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-186">**Example value:** Contoso-IT</span></span>  <br/>                                                                                             |

顯示端點是否位於公司網路內部或外部。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1750">Pair showing if the endpoints were located inside or outside the corporate network based on the subnet mapping and the network connection detail.</span></span>  <br/> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1751">**注意:** 成對專案會以 "--" 分隔。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1751">**Note:** The pairs are separated by '--'.</span></span> ### <a name="notes-on-dimension-data-typeunits"></a><span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1759">[維度] 資料類型/單位的注意事項:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1759">Notes on dimension data type/units:</span></span>

#### <a name="range"></a><span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1760">大量</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1760">Range</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1761">以下列格式顯示以範圍或值群組形式提供的尺寸:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1761">Dimensions that are provided as range or group of values are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1762">_\<排序次序字串\> [\<下限全形\> - \<(含上\>界排他)]_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1762">_\<sort order string\> [\<lower bound inclusive\> - \<upper bound exclusive\>)_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1763">例如, [工期] (分鐘) 維度代表以秒為單位的值, 以值為範圍來表示通話持續時間。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1763">For example, the Duration (Minutes) dimension represents the call duration in seconds with the value reported as a range of values.</span></span>

|||
|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1764">**持續時間 (分鐘)**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1764">**Duration (Minutes)**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1765">**如何解讀**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1765">**How to interpret**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1766">062: [0-0)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1766">062: [0 - 0)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1767">資料流程持續時間 = 0 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1767">Stream duration = 0 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1768">064: [1-2)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1768">064: [1 - 2)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1769">1分鐘 < = 串流持續時間 < 2 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1769">1 minute < = stream duration < 2 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1770">065: [2-3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1770">065: [2 - 3)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1771">2分鐘 < = 資料流程持續時間 < 3 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1771">2 minutes < = stream duration < 3 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1772">066: [3-4)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1772">066: [3 - 4)</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1773">3分鐘 < = 資料流程持續時間 < 4 分鐘</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1773">3 minutes < = stream duration < 4 minutes</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1774">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1774"></span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1775">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1775"></span></span>  <br/> |

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1776"><sort order string>用於在呈現資料時控制排序次序, 並可用於篩選。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1776">The <sort order string> is used to control the sort order when presenting the data and can be used for filtering.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1777">例如, [持續時間 (分鐘)] < "065" 的篩選, 會顯示持續時間少於2分鐘的資料流程 (需要使用前導 "0" 才能如期作業)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1777">For example, a filter on Duration (Minutes) < "065", would show streams with duration less than 2 minutes (The leading '0' is needed for the filter to work as expected).</span></span>

> [!NOTE]
> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1778">排序次序字串的實際值並不重要。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1778">The actual value of the sort order string isn't significant.</span></span>

#### <a name="enumeration-pair"></a><span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1779">列舉對</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1779">Enumeration pair</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1780">以 [列舉] 對提供的尺寸會以下列格式顯示:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1780">Dimensions that are provided as an enumeration pair are shown using the following format:</span></span>

 <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1781">_\<從某個終點開始列舉值\> : \<從其他端點的列舉值\>_</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1781">_\<enumeration value from one end point\> : \<enumeration value from the other endpoint\>_</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1782">列舉值的排序是一致的, 但不會反映第一個或第二個端點的排序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1782">The ordering of the enumeration values is consistent but doesn't reflect ordering of the first or second endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1783">例如, 網路連線詳細資料對會顯示兩個端點的網路連線詳細值:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1783">For example, the Network Connection Detail Pair shows the Network Connection Detail values for the two endpoints:</span></span>

|||
|:-----|:-----|
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1784">**網路連線詳細資料對**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1784">**Network Connection Detail Pair**</span></span> <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1785">**如何解讀**</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1785">**How to interpret**</span></span> <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1786">有線: 有線</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1786">Wired : Wired</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1787">第一和第二個端點都使用有線乙太網連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1787">First and second endpoints both used wired ethernet connections.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1788">有線: wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1788">Wired : wifi</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1789">第一個端點使用有線乙太網連線和第二個端點使用 Wi-fi 連線, 或第二個端點使用的是有線乙太網連線, 而第二個端點使用 Wi-fi 連線。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1789">First endpoint used wired ethernet connection and second endpoint used Wi-Fi connection, or the second endpoint used wired ethernet connection and first endpoint used Wi-Fi connection.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1790">: wifi</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1790">: wifi</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1791">第一個端點使用 WiFi 連線, 而第二個端點所使用的網路連線是未知的, 或第二個端點使用 WiFi 連線, 而第一個端點所使用的網路連線是未知的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1791">First endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the second endpoint is unknown, or the second endpoint used a WiFi connection and the network connection used by the first endpoint is unknown.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1792">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1792"></span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1793">…</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1793"></span></span>  <br/> |

#### <a name="blank-values"></a><span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1794">空白值</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1794">Blank values</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1795">上表列出維度可能為空白的可能原因。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1795">The table above lists possible reasons why a dimension may be blank.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1796">如果 QoE 記錄可用維度為 false, 則許多維度與量值將會是空白的。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1796">Many dimensions and measures will be blank if the QoE Record Available dimension is false.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-1797">這通常是在通話未成功建立時發生。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-1797">This typically occurs when the call wasn't successfully established.</span></span>

|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2149">平均 AppSharing Spoiled 磚總百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2149">Avg AppSharing Spoiled Tile Percent Total</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2150">時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2150">Milliseconds</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2151">已放棄 (例如從 MCU 到檢視器) 資料流程的磚平均百分比, 而不是傳送到遠端對等。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2151">Average of percentage of tiles which are discarded instead of being sent to a remote peer (for example, from the MCU to a viewer) for streams.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2152">已放棄的磚可能是由用戶端與伺服器之間的頻寬限制所造成。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2152">Discarded tiles may be caused by bandwidth restrictions between client and server.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2153">平均 AppSharing 相對單向</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2153">Avg AppSharing Relative OneWay</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2154">秒</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2154">Seconds</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2155">應用程式共用資料流程在端點之間以秒為單位延遲的平均相對單一方式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2155">Average of average relative one way delay between the endpoints in seconds for application sharing streams.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2156">平均 AppSharing RDP 磚處理延遲時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2156">Avg AppSharing RDP Tile Processing Latency</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2157">時間</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2157">Milliseconds</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2158">在每個資料流程的會議服務器上, 在 RDP 堆疊中處理磚的平均延遲時間 (毫秒)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2158">Average of average latency in milliseconds processing tiles on the RDP Stack at the conferencing server for streams.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2159">平均第一個裝置捕獲無法運作事件比率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2159">Avg First Device Capture Not Functioning Event Ratio</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2160">對比度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2160">Ratio</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2161">第一個端點偵測到擷取裝置的通話分數平均值無法正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2161">Average of the fraction of the call that the first endpoint detected the capture device was not working properly.</span></span>  <br/> |

|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2168">平均第二個裝置轉譯無法運作的事件比率</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2168">Avg Second Device Render Not Functioning Event Ratio</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2169">對比度</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2169">Ratio</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2170">第二個端點偵測到轉譯裝置的通話分數平均值無法正常運作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2170">Average of the fraction of the call that the second endpoint detected the render device was not working properly.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2171">媒體由於防火牆 IP 封鎖資料流程計數而失敗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2171">Media Failed Due To Firewall IP Blocked Stream Count</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2172">串流數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2172">Number of streams</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2173">由於網路設備封鎖商務用 Skype 伺服器存取而無法建立的串流數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2173">Number of streams that failed to be established due to network equipment blocking access to Skype for Business servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2174">這些失敗通常表示沒有正確設定 proxy、防火牆或其他網路安全裝置, 以存取 Office 365 中商務用 Skype 所使用的 IP 位址和埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2174">These failures typically indicate a proxy, firewall or other network security device is not correctly configured to access the IP address and ports used by Skype for Business in Office 365.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2175">防火牆 IP 封鎖媒體失敗百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2175">Firewall IP Blocked Media Failure Percentage</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2176">百分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2176">Percentage</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2177">因網路設備封鎖商務用 Skype 伺服器存取而無法建立的資料流程百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2177">Percentage of streams that failed to be established due to network equipment blocking access to Skype for Business servers.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2178">這些失敗通常表示沒有正確設定 proxy、防火牆或其他網路安全裝置, 以存取 Office 365 中商務用 Skype 所使用的 IP 位址和埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2178">These failures typically indicate a proxy, firewall or other network security device is not correctly configured to access the IP address and ports used by Skype for Business in Office 365.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2179">媒體由於防火牆 DPI 資料流程計數而失敗</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2179">Media Failed Due To Firewall DPI Stream Count</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2180">串流數</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2180">Number of streams</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2181">由於深入資料包檢查不允許商務用 Skype 流量而導致由於網路設備封鎖存取而無法建立的串流數。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2181">Number of streams that failed to be established due to network equipment blocking access due to deep packet inspection not allowing Skype for Business traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2182">這些失敗通常表示沒有正確設定 proxy、防火牆或其他網路安全裝置, 以存取 Office 365 中商務用 Skype 所使用的 IP 位址和埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2182">These failures typically indicates a proxy, firewall or other network security device is not correctly configured to access the IP address and ports used by Skype for Business in Office 365.</span></span>  <br/> |
|<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2183">防火牆 DPI 媒體失敗百分比</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2183">Firewall DPI Media Failure Percentage</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2184">百分</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2184">Percentage</span></span>  <br/> |<span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2185">由於深入資料包檢查不允許商務用 Skype 流量而導致由於網路設備封鎖存取而無法建立的資料流程百分比。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2185">Percentage of streams that failed to be established due to network equipment blocking access due to deep packet inspection not allowing Skype for Business traffic.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="29eb2-2186">這些失敗通常表示沒有正確設定 proxy、防火牆或其他網路安全裝置, 以存取 Office 365 中商務用 Skype 所使用的 IP 位址和埠。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="29eb2-2186">These failures typically indicates a proxy, firewall or other network security device is not correctly configured to access the IP address and ports used by Skype for Business in Office 365.</span></span>  <br/> |
